      <script id="results-article-template" type="text/x-handlebars">
       <a href="{{#if permaLink}}{{permaLink}}{{else}}{{permalink}}{{/if}}" class="article {{#if @first}}first{{/if}}">
 	<figure class="image-container">
 		<div class="image" style="background-image: url({{#if imageUrl}}{{imageUrl}}{{else}}{{image}}{{/if}})"></div>
 	</figure>
 	<div class="info-container">
 		<p class="title">{{title}}</p>
 		<p class="byline">
 			{{#if published}}
 				{{#compare type "film"}}
 					{{#if showDate}}
 						<span class="article-date">{{formatDate published "MMMM DD"}}</span>
 					{{/if}}
 				{{else}}
 					<span class="article-date">{{formatDate published "MMMM DD"}}</span>
 				{{/compare}}
 			{{/if}}
 			{{#if author}}<span class="author">by <span>{{author.name}}</span></span>{{/if}}
 			{{#if isRsvpPresent}}
 				<button class="button articleList rsvpButton" data-value="{{rsvpLink}}">RSVP</button>
 			{{/if}}
 		</p>
 
 		{{#if lead}}
 			{{#if showEllipses}}
 				<p class="blurb">{{{ellipsify lead 100}}}</p>
 			{{else}}
 				<p class="blurb">{{{lead}}}</p>
 			{{/if}}
 		{{else}}
 			{{#if showEllipses}}
 				<p class="blurb">{{{ellipsify description 100}}}</p>
 			{{else}}
 				<p class="blurb">{{{description}}}</p>
 			{{/if}}
 		{{/if}}
 
 		<div class="share-toggle" data-type="article">
 			<span class="toggle">{{{svgIcon "icon-add-circle"}}}</span>
 			<div class="controls">
 				<div
 					class="line queue-delegate async"
 					data-type="article"
 					data-id="{{id}}"
 					data-queued-text="{{{svgIcon 'icon-readlist'}}} <span>Remove from Readlist</span>"
 					data-dequeued-text="{{{svgIcon 'icon-readlist'}}} <span>Add to Readlist</span>"
 				>
 					{{{svgIcon 'icon-readlist'}}} <span>Add to Readlist</span>
 				</div>
 				<div class="line share-delegate facebook" data-url="{{permalink}}" data-type="{{type}}" data-share-text="{{title}}">
 					{{{svgIcon "icon-facebook"}}}
 					<span>Share</span>
 				</div>
 				<div class="line share-delegate twitter" data-url="{{permalink}}" data-type="{{type}}" data-share-text="{{title}}">
 					{{{svgIcon "icon-twitter"}}}
 					<span>Tweet</span>
 				</div>
 			</div>
 		</div>
 	</div>
 </a>

       <div class="venue-info-container">
        <div class="venue-summary venue-items">
         <h1 class="title">
          EagleBank Arena
         </h1>
         <div class="summary">
          Located on the campus of Northern Virginia’s George Mason University, EagleBank Arena (formerly the Patriot Center) is a 10,000-seat arena that hosts Mason basketball games, concerts, family shows and commencement ceremonies. Bruce Springsteen, Keith Urban, Bob Dylan, Ricardo Arjona, Enrique Iglesias, the Harlem Globetrotters and Disney on Ice are only a few of the concerts and family shows that have performed at the arena over the past 26 years.
         </div>
         <div class="address">
          <span class="arena">
           This arena is located at
          </span>
          <p>
           4500 Patriot Circle, Fairfax VA 22030
          </p>
          <p>
           Fairfax, VA
          </p>
          <p>
           22030
          </p>

His romantic and fun shows are the only ones where people\r\nregularly jump to their feet and dance in the aisles. It’s not uncommon to see\r\ndevoted American fans laughing, weeping, clapping, dancing and embracing when\r\nthey listen to the beautiful waltzes, film scores, spirituals, musicals, folk\r\nsongs and marches and Andr\u0026eacute;’s precious Stradivarius violin from 1732; his shows\r\nare a perfect mix of thrilling, romantic, festive and emotional melodies\r\ncombined with surprises, balloons, beautiful soloists and of course Andr\u0026eacute;’s\r\ngreat sense of humor. \u003cbr /\u003e\u003cbr /\u003e\r\n\r\n\u0026nbsp;\u003cbr /\u003e\u003cbr /\u003e\r\n\r\n\u003ci\u003e“I’m so excited to return to the\r\nUSA and Canada in September.” says Andr\u0026eacute; Rieu. “People write to me, telling me\r\nthat it takes them two weeks to get back to normal after one of our concerts. It\r\nis simply fantastic to feel this energy and joy every evening.”\u003c/i\u003e\u003cbr /\u003e\u003cbr /\u003e\r\n\r\n\u0026nbsp;\u003cbr /\u003e\u003cbr /\u003e\r\n\r\nAndr\u0026eacute;\r\nand his 60-piece Johann Strauss Orchestra (the largest private orchestra in the\r\nworld) created a global revival in waltz music, staging spectacular\r\nextravaganzas which are second to none. \u0026nbsp;Andr\u0026eacute;’s concerts are a feast not only for the\r\nears but also the eyes! Having received over 500 Platinum Awards, three\r\nClassical Brit Awards for “Album of the Year” and billions of Youtube views,\r\nAndr\u0026eacute; is one of the biggest touring artists in the world. His album “Shall We\r\nDance” is out on Decca Gold. \u003cbr /\u003e\u003cbr /\u003e\r\n\r\n\u0026nbsp;\u003cbr /\u003e\u003cbr /\u003e\r\n\r\n\u003cb\u003eWorld Arena Tour 2018 and Private Life \u003c/b\u003e\u003cbr /\u003e\u003cbr /\u003e\r\n\r\nKnown\r\nto millions around the world as the “King of the Waltz” Andr\u0026eacute; is also a true\r\n“King of Romance”. He has been married for over 40 years and lives with his\r\nwife Marjorie in a historic castle, built in 1452 in his hometown of Maastricht/Netherlands.\r\nThe couple has two sons and five grandchildren. Andr\u0026eacute;’s World Arena Tour 2018 will\r\nhit Europe, Mexico, Israel, the USA and Canada, Argentina and Australia. Mauney\r\nwho is the top-earning athlete in Western sports history with more than $7.2\r\nmillion in career earnings. PBR is part of the Endeavor (formerly WME | IMG)\r\nnetwork. countries. On its elite tour, the organization features the top 35 bull riders in the world and the top bulls in the business. The televised 25th PBR: Unleash The Beast, along with the PBR Real Time Pain Relief Velocity Tour (RVT), the PBR Touring Pro Division (TPD) and the PBR’s international circuits in Australia, Brazil, Canada and Mexico have paid $184 million in earnings to its athletes. Thirty bull riders have earned more than $1 million, including two-time PBR World Champion J.B. Mauney who is the top-earning athlete in Western sports history with more than $7.2 million in career earnings. PBR is part of the Endeavor (formerly WME | IMG) network.     // Include helpers/share-toggle, which is MSE only event listener (for now)
 define('mastheads/monumental-network', ['mastheads/ticker', 'lib/URI', 'helpers/share-toggle', 'helpers/login'], function(tickerModule, URI) {
 	function tmpModule(defaults) {
 		Module.call(this, {
 			mod: 'mastheads/monumental-network',
 			api: '/apis/search/typeahead.json',
 			throttleTiming: 100,
 			dataLimit: 5,
 			currentCall: null,
 			tickerObject: null,
 			eventListener: null,
 			templates: {
 				article: Handlebars.compile($('#results-article-template').html()),
 				event: Handlebars.compile($('#results-event-template').html())
 			},
 			siteSkinAd: null,
 			prestitialAd: null,
 			dom: {
 				body: null,
 				searchIcon: null,
 				mobileSearchIcon: null,
 				searchContainer: null,
 				searchResultsContainer: null,
 				globalNav: null,
 				globalToggle: null,
 				globalNavClose: null,
 				mobileNavTop: null,
 				mobileNavBottom: null,
 				mobileNavToggle: null,
 				iframeAuthWidget: null,
 				tickerContainer: null
 			},
 
 			postProcess: function() {
 				console.log(this.label(), 'Post Process');
 				$.removeCookie('rsvp_return_url');
 				$.removeCookie('subscription-plan-type');
 
 				this.dom.body = $('body');
 				this.dom.searchContainer = this.div.find('.typeahead-search-container');
 				this.dom.searchIcon = this.div.find('.masthead-section.search-container, .typeahead-search-close-icon');
 				this.dom.searchResultsContainer = this.div.find('.typeahead-search-results');
 				this.dom.globalNav = this.div.find('.large-version .global-nav');
 				this.dom.globalToggle = this.div.find('.link-more');
 
 				this.dom.searchIcon.on('click', $.proxy(this.searchContainerToggle, this));
 				this.dom.globalToggle.on('click', $.proxy(this.globalNavToggle, this));
 
 				this.dom.globalNav.hover(
 					$.proxy(function() {
 						this.dom.globalNav.addClass('js-mousein');
 					}, this),
 					$.proxy(function() {
 						this.dom.globalNav.removeClass('js-mousein');
 					}, this)
 				);
 
 				this.dom.globalNavClose = this.div.find('.global-nav-top .close');
 				this.dom.globalNavClose.on('click', $.proxy(function() {
 					this.dom.globalNav.removeClass('expanded');
 					var toggleText = this.dom.globalToggle.find('.toggle-text');
 					toggleText.text(toggleText.attr('data-closed-text'));
 					this.dom.globalToggle.removeClass('expanded');
 					this.dom.globalNav.css({
 						height: '0px'
 					});
 				}, this));
 
 				Snag.constants.site.entitlementCheckRequired = this.setup.data.entitlementCheckRequired;
 
 				// Calculate expanded global nav height
 				var expandedHeight = 0;
 				var globalNavTop = this.dom.globalNav.find('.global-nav-top');
 				var globalNavSites = this.dom.globalNav.find('.sites');
 				var expandedHeight = globalNavTop.outerHeight(true) + globalNavSites.outerHeight(true);
 				this.dom.globalNav.attr('data-expanded-height', expandedHeight);
 
 				// Mobile nav
 				this.dom.mobileNavTop = this.div.find('.mobile-nav-top');
 				this.dom.mobileNavBottom = this.div.find('.mobile-nav-bottom');
 				this.dom.mobileNavToggle = this.div.find('.mobile-nav-toggle');
 				this.dom.mobileSearchIcon = this.div.find('#mobile-header-search-handle');
 
 				this.dom.mobileSearchContainer = this.div.find('#mobile-typeahead-container');
 				this.dom.mobileSearchResultsContainer = this.div.find('#mobile-typeahead-results-container');
 				this.dom.mobileTypeaheadInput = this.div.find('#mobile-typeahead-search');
 
 				this.dom.mobileNavToggle.on('click', $.proxy(this.mobileNavViewSwitch, this));
 				this.dom.mobileNavBottom.on('click', '.nav-site-toggle', $.proxy(this.onMobileNavSiteToggleClick, this));
 				this.dom.mobileSearchIcon.on('click', $.proxy(this.mobileSearchContainerToggle, this));
 
 				this.dom.typeaheadInput = this.div.find('#header-search-form input');
 				this.dom.typeaheadInput.on('keyup', _.throttle($.proxy(this.makeQuery, this), this.throttleTiming));
 
 				// Mobile Menu
 				this.div.find('.mobile-menu').on('click', $.proxy(function() {
 					this.dom.mobileSearchContainer.addClass('hide');
 					this.dom.mobileSearchIcon.removeClass('active');
 					this.dom.mobileSearchContainer.removeClass('expanded');
 					this.dom.body.toggleClass('expanded-nav');
 				}, this));
 				this.div.find('.toggle-user-menu').on('click', function() {
 					this.dom.body.toggleClass('expanded-user-menu');
 				});
 
 				// Sync Snag user with masthead user (if they are the same user)
 				if (this.setup.data.user && this.setup.data.user.id === Snag.constants.user.id) {
 					$.extend(Snag.constants.user, this.setup.data.user);
 				}
 
 				this.listen('window:message', $.proxy(this.onMessage, this));
 				this.listen('login:success', $.proxy(this.loginSuccess, this));
 				this.listen('newPoints:added', $.proxy(this.getTotalPointsForUser, this));
 				// John The Ticker (who is John?)
 				if (this.setup.data.contentIdMap && this.setup.data.contentIdMap.ticker) {
 					this.dom.tickerContainer = this.div.find("#ticker");
 					this.tickerObject = new tickerModule({ contentId: this.setup.data.contentIdMap.ticker });
 					this.tickerObject.div = this.dom.tickerContainer;
 					this.tickerObject.postProcess();
 				} else {
 					this.dom.body.addClass('ticker-none');
 				}
 
 				if(Snag.constants.user.loggedIn) {
 					this.div.addClass('logged-in');
 					this.showFavoriteTeams();
 				}
 
 
 				// Log out listener
 				this.div.find('.log-out-link').on('click', $.proxy(function(event) {
 					event.preventDefault();
 					Snag.SetLoading();
 					this.dom.iframeAuthWidget.postMessage('viewlift|login:logout', '*');
 					setTimeout(Snag.logout, 200);
 					return false;
 				}, this));
 
 				// Overwrite Snag.helpers.login.modalLogin()
 				Snag.helpers.login.modalLogin = Snag.helpers.login.modalRegister = $.proxy(function(options) {
 					Snag.Modal(
 						'',
 						'<iframe class="embedded-sign-in" src="' + ((this.setup.config['networkDomain']) ? this.setup.config['networkDomain'] : '') + '/embed/sign-in" frameborder="0"></iframe>',
 						{
 							className: 'modal-login'
 						}
 					);
 					var iframe = $(document).find("#modal .modal-body iframe");
 					$(function(){
 						var lastHeight = iframe.height(), curHeight = lastHeight;
 						iframe.load(function(e){
 							iframe.css({ height : iframe.contents().height() + 'px' });
 							var resizeTimer = setInterval( function() {
 								try { curHeight = iframe.contents().height(); }
 								catch(e) { clearInterval(resizeTimer); return 0; }
 								if ( curHeight != lastHeight ) iframe.css({ height : ( lastHeight = curHeight ) + 'px' });
 							},250);
 						});
 					});
 
 					// Refresh the page after login if `refresh: true`
 					if (options && options.refresh) {
 						this.listen('login:success', Snag.ForwardUrl);
 					}
 				}, this);
 				this.listen('login:success', $.proxy(this.onRegistration, this));
 
 				// [ASYNC] Get Rewards/Points listener
 				// [TEMP] Allow for production turning off
 				if(typeof(this.setup['noRewards']) == 'undefined') {
 
 					require(['helpers/events/monumental-network'], $.proxy(function(eventListenerModule) {
 						console.log(this.label() + 'Loaded MSE reward points helper');
 						this.eventListener = new eventListenerModule();
 						this.eventListener.div = this.div;
 						this.eventListener.setup = this.setup;
 						this.eventListener.postProcess();
 					}, this));
 				}
 				// Sends back site object map of point activity IDs
 				this.listen('rewards:getPoints', $.proxy(this.getPoints, this));
 
 				//intializing subscription file(billing/monumental-network)
 				if (this.setup.data.entitlementCheckRequired) {
 					require(['billing/monumental-network'], $.proxy(function(accountManagement){
 						var accountManage = new accountManagement();
 						accountManage.div = this.div;
 						accountManage.setup = this.setup;
 						accountManage.postProcess();
 					}, this))
 				}
 
 				// Render RSVP button on pages
 				this.renderRSVP();
 
 				// Add encrypted key to shop.monumental.. links for aramark
 				this.setShopUrls();
 
 				// show personalization prompt if neccesary
 				if (
 					this.setup.data.user &&
 					localStorage.getItem('needsPersonalization') &&
 					window.location.pathname !== '/thank-you'
 				) {
 					this.initialPersonalization();
 				}
 			},
 
 			isValidSubscription: function(){
 				if(Snag.constants.user.subscribed || Snag.constants.user.validSubscription){
 					return true;
 				}
 				for(var i = 0; i < Snag.page.data.length; i++){
 					if(Snag.page.data[i].data !== undefined){
 						if(Snag.page.data[i].data.user !== undefined){
 							return Snag.page.data[i].data.user.validSubscription;
 						}
 					}
 				}
 				return false;
 			},
 
 			newTab: function(url) {
 				var form = document.createElement("form");
 				form.method = "GET";
 				form.action = url;
 				form.target = "_blank";
 				document.body.appendChild(form);
 				form.submit();
 				form.remove();
 			},
 
 			renderRSVP: function(){
 				var template = Handlebars.compile($('#splash-screen-template').html())
 				$(document).on('click touchstart', '.rsvpButton', $.proxy(function(event){
 					event.preventDefault();
 					event.stopPropagation();
 					var href = event.target.attributes['data-value'].nodeValue;
 					$.cookie('rsvp_return_url', href);
 					if(!Snag.constants.user.loggedIn){
 						event.preventDefault();
 						$('.modal-back').hide();
 						$.extend(this.setup.rsvpSplash, { rsvp: true, signInPrompt: true });
 						var renderedTemplate = template(this.setup.rsvpSplash);
 						Snag.Modal('', renderedTemplate, { className: 'no-header splash-screen-modal' })
 					}else{
 						if(!this.isValidSubscription()){
 							event.preventDefault();
 							$('.modal-back').hide();
 							$.extend(this.setup.rsvpSplash, { rsvp: true });
 							var renderedTemplate = template(this.setup.rsvpSplash);
 							Snag.Modal('', renderedTemplate, { className: 'no-header splash-screen-modal' })
 						}else{
 							$.removeCookie('rsvp_return_url');
 							this.newTab(href);
 							// window.open(href, "_blank");
 						}
 					}
 					$('.rsvp button.rsvp-sign-in').on('click', $.proxy(function(event){
 						event.preventDefault();
 						Snag.helpers.login.modalLogin();
 					}));
 					$('.rsvp button.mse-subscription').on('click', $.proxy(function(event){
 						$.cookie('subscription-plan-type', 'YEAR');
 					}));
 				}, this));
 			},
 
 			showFavoriteTeams: function() {
 				var favoriteTeams = this.setup.data.favoriteTeamTags;
 
 				$.ajax({
 					url: '/apis/follow/getcontent.json?',
 					type: 'get',
 					data : {
 						user_id : this.setup.data.user.id,
 						timestamp : "Snag.constants.site.apiSignature.timestamp",
 						access_key : "Snag.constants.site.apiSignature.accessKey",
 						signature : "Snag.constants.site.apiSignature.signature"
 					},
 					success: $.proxy(function(data) {
 						var tags = data.content.tags;
 						var blogModules = $('.featured-blog-module');
 						var newsModules = $('.team-info-container');
 
 						newsModules.each($.proxy(function(index, _elem) {
 							var elem = $(_elem);
 							var teamId = elem.data("team-id");
 							if (teamId != undefined)
 							{
 								for ( i = 0; i < tags.length; i++) {
 									if (tags[i].id == teamId) {
 										break;
 									}
 								}
 
 								if (i == tags.length) {
 									elem.addClass("hide");
 								}
 							}
 						}));
 					}, this),
 				});
 			},
 
 			searchContainerToggle: function(event) {
 				event.preventDefault();
 				this.dom.typeaheadInput.val('');
 				this.dom.searchContainer.toggleClass('expanded');
 				this.dom.searchResultsContainer.html('').parent().toggleClass('expanded');
 				this.dom.searchIcon.toggleClass('active');
 				if(this.currentCall != null) {
 					this.currentCall.abort();
 				}
 				if(this.dom.searchContainer.hasClass('expanded')) {
 					this.dom.typeaheadInput.focus();
 				}
 				return false;
 			},
 			mobileSearchContainerToggle: function(event) {
 				event.preventDefault();
 
 				this.dom.mobileTypeaheadInput.val('');
 				this.dom.mobileSearchContainer.toggleClass('expanded');
 				this.dom.mobileSearchContainer.toggleClass('hide');
 				this.dom.mobileSearchIcon.toggleClass('active');
 				if(this.currentCall != null) {
 					this.currentCall.abort();
 				}
 				if(this.dom.mobileSearchContainer.hasClass('expanded')) {
 					this.dom.mobileTypeaheadInput.focus();
 				}
 				return false;
 			},
 			globalNavToggle: function() {
 				this.dom.globalNav.toggleClass('expanded');
 				var toggleText = this.dom.globalToggle.find('.toggle-text');
 
 				if(this.dom.globalNav.hasClass('expanded')) {
 					toggleText.text(toggleText.attr('data-opened-text'));
 					this.dom.globalToggle.addClass('expanded');
 					this.dom.globalNav.css({
 						height: this.dom.globalNav.attr('data-expanded-height') + 'px'
 					});
 				}
 
 				else {
 					toggleText.text(toggleText.attr('data-closed-text'));
 					this.dom.globalToggle.removeClass('expanded');
 					this.dom.globalNav.css({
 						height: '0px'
 					});
 				}
 			},
 			mobileNavViewSwitch: function() {
 				if(this.dom.mobileNavTop.hasClass('active')) {
 					this.dom.mobileNavTop.removeClass('active');
 					this.dom.mobileNavBottom.addClass('active');
 					this.dom.mobileNavToggle.addClass('expanded').find('.text').text(this.dom.mobileNavToggle.attr('data-expanded-text'));
 				}
 
 				else {
 					this.dom.mobileNavTop.addClass('active');
 					this.dom.mobileNavBottom.removeClass('active');
 					this.dom.mobileNavToggle.removeClass('expanded').find('.text').text(this.dom.mobileNavToggle.attr('data-collapsed-text'));
 				}
 			},
 			onMobileNavSiteToggleClick: function(event) {
 				event.preventDefault();
 				var target = $(event.target).closest('.nav-site-toggle');
 				var parent = target.parent();
 				parent.siblings().removeClass('active');
 				parent.toggleClass('active');
 				return false;
 			},
 			makeQuery: function(event) {
 
 				// No special keys
 				var ignoreCodes = [37, 38, 39, 16, 17, 18, 91]
 				if(_.indexOf(ignoreCodes, event.keyCode) > -1) {
 					return false;
 				}
 
 				if(this.currentCall != null) {
 					this.currentCall.abort();
 				}
 
 				var searchTerm = this.dom.typeaheadInput.val();
 				if(searchTerm.length > 2) {
 					this.currentCall = $.ajax({
 						url: this.api,
 						type: 'get',
 						data: {
 							searchTerm: searchTerm,
 							limit: this.dataLimit
 						},
 						complete: $.proxy(this.callComplete, this),
 						success: $.proxy(this.handleResults, this)
 					});
 				} else {
 					this.dom.searchResultsContainer.html('');
 				}
 			},
 			callComplete: function() {
 				this.currentCall = null;
 			},
 			handleResults: function(data) {
 				console.log(this.label(), data.results);
 				this.dom.searchResultsContainer.html('');
 				for(var i in data.results) {
 					var result = data.results[i];
 					if ((result.contentType == 'article') || (result.contentType == 'film')) {
 						this.dom.searchResultsContainer.append(this.templates.article(result));
 					}
 					console.log(result);
 				}
 //				this.dom.resultsContainer.html(this.template(data)).addClass('expanded');
 			},
 			onMessage: function(event, data) {
 				console.log(this.label() + ' onMessage', data);
 				if(_.isString(data.data)) {
 					if(data.data == 'login:embedded-login-click') {
 						Snag.helpers.login.modalLogin();
 					} else if(data.data == 'login:announce-self') {
 						console.log(this.label() + ' Found iframe');
 						this.dom.iframeAuthWidget = data.source;
 
 						// Out-of-sync login situation
 						if(data['loggedIn'] === true && Snag.constants.user.loggedIn === false) {
 							this.dom.iframeAuthWidget.postMessage('viewlift|login:sync', '*');
 							this.div.addClass('logged-in');
 							Snag.constants.user.loggedIn = true;
 						} else {
 							// Pull missing user properties from the masthead object to the Snag object
 							$.extend(Snag.constants.user, this.setup.data.user);
 						}
 					}else if(data.data == 'login:success' || data.data == 'login:sync:success') {
 						this.loginSuccess(data);
 						this.broadcast('login:success');
 					}else if(data.data == 'site-skin:parameters') {
 						this.initSkinAd(data);
 					}else if(data.data == 'site-skin:markup') {
 						this.addSkinAdMarkup(data);
 					}else if(data.data == 'Dfp:PrestialAd:Parameters') {
 						this.initPrestitialAd(data);
 					} else if(data.data == 'points:added') {
 						this.dom.iframeAuthWidget.postMessage('viewlift|points:added', "*");
 					}
 				}
 			},
 			initPrestitialAd: function(data) {
 				console.log(this.label() + 'initPrestitialAd', data);
 				if(data['image']){
 					require(['advertising/prestitial-ad'], function(prestitialAdModule){
 							$('.viewlift-prestitial-ad').show();
 							this.prestitialAd = new prestitialAdModule();
 							this.prestitialAd.div = this.div;
 							this.prestitialAd.setup = this.setup;
 							this.prestitialAd.viewURLPrefix = data['viewURLPrefix'] || '';
 							this.prestitialAd.clickThroughUrl = data['clickThroughUrl'] || '';
 							this.prestitialAd.image = data['image'] || '';
 							this.prestitialAd.url = data['url'] || '';
 							this.prestitialAd.timeDuration = data['duration']||10;
 							this.prestitialAd.overlayBackgroundColor = data['overlayBackgroundColor'] || '';
 							this.prestitialAd.postProcess();
 					}, function(error){
 						console.log('Failed to load prestitial ad module!');
 						$('.viewlift-prestitial-ad').hide();
 					});
 				}else{
 					console.log('ad image for prestitial-ad missing from data(DFP)');
 					$('.viewlift-prestitial-ad').hide();
 				}
 			},
 			loginSuccess: function(data) {
 				console.log(this.label() + 'loginSuccess()', data);
 				try {
 					this.dom.iframeAuthWidget.postMessage('viewlift|login:success', '*');
 				} catch (e) {
 					console.error(e);
 				}
 				if($('.modal-dialog').hasClass('start') == false){
 					Snag.RemoveModal();
 				}
 				this.div.addClass('logged-in');
 
 				if(_.isObject(data['user'])) {
 					if(data.user.subscribed == "true"){
 						var _url = $.cookie('rsvp_return_url') || null;
 						if(_url !== null){
 							$.removeCookie('rsvp_return_url');
 							this.newTab(_url);
 						}
 					}
 					Snag.constants.user = data.user;
 					Snag.constants.user.loggedIn = true;
 				}
 
 				// Reload iframeAuthWidgets
 				$('.js-masthead-auth').each(function (i, iframe) {
 					iframe.contentWindow.location.reload();
 				});
 
 				// Sync login if:
 				// 		1. we know the token cookie is present
 				// 		2. we know this is a sub-site within the network
 				if(this.setup.config['networkDomain'] && _.isString(data['token'])) {
 					Snag.SetLoading();
 					$.ajax({
 						url: '/apis/svod/token/' + data.token,
 						type: 'get',
 						data: {
 							site: Snag.constants.site.internalName,
 							rememberMe: true
 						},
 						complete: function() {
 							Snag.UnsetLoading();
 						},
 						success: $.proxy(function(data) {
 							console.log('Logged In', data);
 							this.setShopUrls(data);
 						},this),
 						error: function() {
 							console.warn('Not Logged In', arguments);
 						}
 					});
 				}
 
 				this.setShopUrls(data);
 			},
 
 			onRegistration: function() {
 				if (Snag.constants.user.newRegistration) {
 					// set some flag that says that you are new registree
 					localStorage.setItem('needsPersonalization', true);
 				}
 			},
 
 			initialPersonalization: function () {
 				localStorage.removeItem('needsPersonalization');
 				sessionStorage.setItem('initPersonalization', true);
 				$.when(Snag.Confirm('Personalize Your Experience', 'Would you like to add your favorite players, teams, and tags to your profile? It will allow you to get specific content and instant updates about the things you are most interested in.'))
 				.then(function() {
 					window.location = 'https://www.monumentalsportsnetwork.com/user/personalization';
 				});
 			},
 
 			initSkinAd: function(data) {
 				console.log(this.label() + 'initSkinAd', data);
 				require(['advertising/site-skin'], function(siteSkinModule){
 					this.siteSkinAd = new siteSkinModule();
 					this.siteSkinAd.div = this.div;
 					this.siteSkinAd.setup = this.setup;
 					this.siteSkinAd.viewURLPrefix = data['viewURLPrefix'] || '';
 					this.siteSkinAd.image = data['image'] || '';
 					this.siteSkinAd.url = data['url'] || '';
 
 					this.siteSkinAd.postProcess();
 				}, function(error){
 					console.log('Failed to load skin ad module!');
 				});
 			},
 			addSkinAdMarkup: function(data) {
 				if(_.isString(data['markup'])) {
 					$('#site-skin').append($(data.markup));
 				}
 			},
 
 			// Reflect when asked
 			getPoints: function() {
 				var points = this.setup.data['pointActivities'] || [];
 				this.broadcast('rewards:setPoints', { points: points });
 			},
 
 			// Pass UUID to Monumental Shop url
 			setShopUrls: function (data) {
 				var uuid;
 				var user;
 
 				if (checkNested(data, 'user', 'id')) {
 					user = data.user;
 					uuid = data.user.id;
 				} else if (checkNested(this.setup.data, 'user', 'id')) {
 					user = this.setup.data.user;
 					uuid = this.setup.data.user.id;
 				} else {
 					return false;
 				}
 
 				if (!user.validSubscription) {
 					return false;
 				}
 
 				$.ajax({
 					url: '/apis/user/svod/encryptUUID',
 					type: 'get',
 					data: {
 						uuID: uuid
 					},
 					success: $.proxy(function(data) {
 						// Select all anchor tags with href containing the string "shop.monumental"
 						var $links = $('a[href*="shop.monumental"]');
 						var token = data.data;
 
 						$links.each(function (i, link) {
 							// Get Old URL
 							var oldURL = $(link).attr('href');
 
 							// Modify URL
 							var newURL = URI(oldURL)
 								.domain("monumentalsportsnetwork.com") // make sure domain is monumentalsportsnetwork.com not monumentalsports.com
 								.addSearch("ViewLift_Token", token); // add ViewLift_Token
 
 							// Set Url
 							$(link).attr('href', newURL);
 						})
 					}, this),
 				});
 			}
 		});
 	}
 	return tmpModule;
 });
 define('collections/events', ['lib/fullcalendar.min', 'lib/jquery.scrollTo-1.4.6.min'], function() {
 	function tmpModule(defaults) {
 		Module.call(this, {
 			mod: 'collections/events',
 			dom: {
 				body: null,
 				eventsSlider: null,
 				eventsContainer: null,
 				calendar: null,
 				calendarContainer: null,
 				allCalendarTDs: null,
 				mobileCalendarToggle: null,
 				mobileCalendarCloseButton: null,
 				eventsFilter: null,
 				filterInput: null,
 				dropdownButtons: null
 			},
 			lazyLoad: true,
 			limit: 999,
 			numEventsLoaded: 0,
 			usePortrait: false,
 			sticky: false,
 			stickyTopOffset : {
 				desktop : -1,
 				mobile : -1
 			},
 			currentCalendar: {
 				start: null,
 				end: null,
 				firstDayOfMonth: null,
 				numDays: 0,
 				calendarObject : null,
 				displayCalendar : null,
 				events: []
 			},
 			selectedDate: '',
 			usePortrait : false,
 			activeFilters: {},
 			eventTemplate: null,
 			filtersListTemplate: null,
 			venueHandles: {},
 			eventTypeFilter : "",
 			
 			postProcess: function() {
 				console.log(this.label() + ' Post Process');
 				
 				// DOM CACHING
 				this.dom.body = $('body');
 				this.dom.eventsFilter = this.div.find('.events-filter');
 				this.dom.dropdownButtons = this.div.find('.filter-dropdown');
 				this.dom.filterInput = this.div.find('input[name="q"]');
 				this.dom.mobileCalendarToggle = this.div.find('.mobile-calendar-toggle');
 				this.dom.mobileCalendarCloseButton = this.div.find('.mobile-calendar-off');
 				this.dom.eventsContainer = this.div.find('.events-container');
 				this.dom.eventsSlider = this.div.find('.events-slider');
 				this.dom.loadMoreButton = this.div.find('.load-more a');
 				this.dom.calendarContainer = this.div.find('.calendar-container');
 				this.dom.calendar = this.div.find('.calendar');
 				this.dom.spinner = this.div.find('.loading-spinner');
 				this.dom.noData = this.div.find('.no-data');
 				
 				// Stanza handles
 				this.venueHandles = {
 					'default': '@monumental',
 					'Verizon Center': '@monumental',
 					'EagleBank Arena': '@eaglebankarena'
 				};
 				
 				//setting up current date
 				this.currentDate = moment();
 				this.currentCalendar.start = moment(new Date(Date.apply(null, new Date())).setDate(1));
 				this.currentCalendar.end = moment().add(1, 'month');
 				this.currentCalendar.numDays = Math.floor(this.currentCalendar.end.diff(this.currentCalendar.start) / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24));
 				this.currentCalendar.displayCalendar = (this.dom.calendarContainer.css("display") == "none" ? false : true);
 				this.selectedDate = this.currentDate;
 				
 				//init calendar
 				this.currentCalendar.calendarObject = this.dom.calendar.html('').fullCalendar({
 					height: 'auto',
 					header: {
 						left: 'prev',
 						center: 'title',
 						right: 'next'
 					},
 					dayClick: $.proxy(this.dayClick, this),
 					viewRender: $.proxy(this.viewRender, this)
 				});
 				
 				// Initialize Add-To-Calendar buttons
 				this.initAddToCalendar();
 				
 				// Compile Templates
 				this.eventTemplate = Handlebars.compile($('#event-template').html());
 				if(this.dom.eventsFilter.length != 0){
 					this.filtersListTemplate = Handlebars.compile($('#filters-list').html());
 				}
 				
 				// Overrides
 				var options = this.div.find('.options');
 				if(options.length > 0) {
 					if(options.attr('data-lazy-load')) {
 						if(options.attr('data-lazy-load') === 'true') {
 							this.lazyLoad = true;
 						} else {
 							this.lazyLoad = false;
 						}
 					}
 					if(options.attr('data-sticky')) {
 						if(options.attr('data-sticky') === 'true') {
 							this.sticky = true;
 						} else {
 							this.sticky = false;
 						}
 					}
 					if(options.attr('data-limit')) {
 						this.limit = parseInt(options.attr('data-limit'));
 					}
 				}
 				
 				//Event Filtering by Type
 				if (this.setup.eventTypeFilter)
 					this.eventTypeFilter = this.setup.eventTypeFilter;
 				
 				if (this.setup.displayDateSeparator)
 					this.displayDateSeparator = this.setup.displayDateSeparator;
 				
 				
 				$(window).resize($.proxy(this.resize, this));
 				
 				this.dom.loadMoreButton.on('click', $.proxy(this.loadMore, this));
 				
 				this.dom.mobileCalendarToggle.on('click', $.proxy(this.onMobileCalendarToggleClick, this));
 				this.dom.mobileCalendarCloseButton.on('click', $.proxy(this.onMobileCalendarToggleClick, this));
 				
 				// Event Binding
 				this.dom.filterInput.on('keyup paste input', $.proxy(this.onKeyUp, this));
 				this.dom.dropdownButtons.on('click', $.proxy(this.onDropdownClick, this));
 				this.div.on('change', '.filter-checkbox', $.proxy(this.onFilterChoiceClick, this));
 				
 				//Portrait
 				if (this.setup.usePortrait != undefined)
 					this.usePortrait = this.setup.usePortrait;
 				
 				this.initFilters();
 				//element sticky
 				if (this.sticky && window.innerWidth >= 600) {
 					this.makeSticky(this.dom.calendarContainer.find(".calendar-placeholder"));
 					this.makeSticky(this.dom.mobileCalendarToggle);
 				}
 				
 				// Temporary hotfix
 				if (this.setup.data.filters.venues.length === 0) {
 					this.dom.dropdownButtons.filter('[data-filter=venues]').remove();
 				}
 				
 				this.callForEvents();
 			},
 			callForEvents: function() {
 				// All relevent venues (ignoring filter)
 				var venues = _.map(this.filters.venues, 'id');
 				var toDate = moment(this.currentCalendar.end).add(1, 'month');
 				var requestData = {
 					fromDate: this.currentCalendar.start.format('MM-DD-YYYY'),
 					toDate: toDate.format('MM-DD-YYYY'),
 					venue: venues.join(','),
 					limit: 999
 				};
 				
 				if (this.eventTypeFilter != "")
 					requestData.type = this.eventTypeFilter;
 				
 				this.dom.eventsContainer.addClass("hide");
 				this.dom.noData.addClass("hide");
 				this.dom.spinner.removeClass("hide");
 				$.ajax({
 					url: '/apis/events.json',
 					type: 'get',
 					data: requestData,
 					success: $.proxy(this.updateCalendar, this)
 				});
 			},
 			updateCalendar: function(data) {
 				console.log(this.label() + ' Update Calendar', data);
 				
 				this.dom.calendarContainer.removeClass("hide");
 				this.currentCalendar.displayCalendar = (this.dom.calendarContainer.css("display") == "none" ? false : true);
 				this.dom.eventsContainer.removeClass("hide");
 				this.dom.spinner.addClass("hide");
 				
 				if (this.dom.calendarContainer.css("display") != "none") {
 					this.currentCalendar.calendarObject.fullCalendar('render');
 				}
 				
 				if(data.events) {
 					// Collect each event and order by date
 					this.currentCalendar.events = data.events;
 					_.forEach(this.currentCalendar.events, function(event){
 						event.moment = new moment(event.eventDate);
 						event.dateStr = event.moment.format('YYYY-MM-DD');
 					});
 					
 					this.styleCalendar();
 					this.processEvents(data.events);
 					this.displayEvents();
 					
 					return false;
 				}
 				else {
 					console.warn(this.label() + ' Bad data');
 				}
 			},
 			processEvents: function(events) {
 				
 				_.forEach(events, $.proxy(function(event){
 					
 					// Set date properties
 					var eventDateObj = moment(event.eventDate);
 					event.headerDate = eventDateObj.format("DD");
 					event.headerWeekDay = eventDateObj.format("MMM");
 					event.isToday = eventDateObj.isSame(this.currentDate, 'day');
 					
 					// Set portrait properties
 					if(this.usePortrait && event.eventPortraitImage) {
 						event.usePortrait = true;
 						event.eventImage = event.eventPortraitImage;
 					} else {
 						event.usePortrait = false;
 					}
 					
 					// Set Stanza handle
 					event.handle = this.venueHandles[event.venue];
 					
 					// Render event template
 					event.element = $(this.eventTemplate(event));
 					
 				}, this));
 			},
 			
 			displayEvents: function(options) {
 				console.log(this.label() + ' Display Events ' + this.currentDate.format('MM-DD-YYYY'));
 				options = options || {};
 				var appendMore = (options && options.appendMore) ? options.appendMore : false;
 				var showAll = (options && options.showAll) ? options.showAll : false;
 				var numShown = 0;
 				var currentDay = null;
 				var currentMonth = null;
 				var containerToAppend = this.dom.eventsSlider;
 				var dateObj;
 				var headerText;
 				var monthText = "";
 				// Object to determine if a filter category has all options checked
 				var filters = this.filters;
 				var filterOptions = _.reduce(this.activeFilters, function(result, value, key){
 					result[key] = (value.length !== Object.keys(filters[key]).length);
 					return result;
 				}, {});
 				
 				if (!appendMore) {
 					this.numEventsLoaded = 0;
 					this.dom.eventsSlider.empty();
 				}
 				
 				_.forEach(this.currentCalendar.events, $.proxy(function(event){
 					
 					if (showAll || numShown < this.limit) {
 						
 						// Does event match all filters?
 						if (this.eventFilter(event, filterOptions) === true) {
 							// If event is on a new day, create the day header
 							if (((this.lazyLoad && !appendMore) || this.displayDateSeparator) && event.dateStr != currentDay) {
 								currentDay = event.dateStr;
 								dateObj = new moment(event.eventDate);
 								if (currentMonth != dateObj.format('MMMM'))
 								{
 									console.log(currentMonth +" "+dateObj.format('MMMM'));
 									currentMonth = dateObj.format('MMMM');
 									monthText = currentMonth+", "
 								}else{
 									monthText = "";
 								}
 								headerText = dateObj.format('dddd DD');
 								this.dom.eventsSlider.append('<h2 class="events-day-header">' + monthText + headerText + '</h2><div class="events-day-container"></div>');
 								containerToAppend = this.dom.eventsSlider.find(".events-day-container:last");
 							}
 							// Append event to the current day header
 							containerToAppend.append(event.element);
 							numShown += 1;
 						}
 					}
 				}), this);
 				
 				// If we're in lazyLoad mode, there are many events shown, scroll user to top
 				if(this.lazyLoad && !appendMore) {
 					setTimeout(function() {
 						$(document).scrollTo(0, 0, { duration: 120 });
 					}, 50);
 				}
 				
 				this.checkDisplayState();
 			},
 			
 			//Make Sticky
 			makeSticky : function( _elem ) {
 				$(function(){
 					var elem = $(_elem);
 					var topOffset = -1;
 					var visible = (elem.is(':hidden') || elem.css('display') == 'none' ? false : true);
 					if (visible)
 					{
 						elem.css( { position : "relative" } );	
 						topOffset = elem.offset().top - $(".padded-section").offset().top;
 						elem.css( { position : "" } );	
 					}
 					
 					function checkSticky(e){
 						var _visible = (elem.is(':hidden') || elem.css('display') == 'none' ? false : true);
 						if (visible != _visible)
 						{
 							if ((_visible) && (topOffset==-1))
 							{
 								elem.css( { position : "relative" } );	
 								topOffset = elem.offset().top - $(".padded-section").offset().top;
 								elem.css( { position : "" } );	
 							}
 							visible = _visible;
 						}
 						
 						if ( topOffset >= 0 )
 						if ((topOffset - $(document).scrollTop() <= 0) && (topOffset != -1))
 						{
 							elem.addClass("sticky-calendar");
 						}else{
 							elem.removeClass("sticky-calendar");
 						}
 					};
 					$(window).resize($.proxy(checkSticky,this));
 					$(document).scroll($.proxy(checkSticky,this));
 				});
 			},
 			initFilters: function(){
 				// Set Up Filters (easily extensible)
 				// This functionality should be able to work with any number of future filters as long as:
 				//   the filters come in this.setup.data.filters with the same structure as current ones
 				//   the filter category should be plural and events should have data attribut that is singular (must be same string as category minus the last letter)
 				//     ie: "venues" and "venue"
 				this.filters = _.reduce(this.setup.data.filters, function(newFilter, category, key){
 					newFilter[key] = _.reduce(category, function(newFilterObj, categoryValue, categoryKey){
 						newFilterObj[categoryKey] = {
 							name: categoryValue.name,
 							checked: true
 						};
 						return newFilterObj;
 					}, {});
 					return newFilter;
 				}, {});
 				
 				// Set Arrays of Active Filters
 				this.activeFilters = _.reduce(this.filters, function(result, value, key){
 					result[key] = _.map(value, 'name');
 					return result;
 				}, {});
 			},
 			onDropdownClick: function(event) {
 				event.preventDefault();
 				var $element = $(event.target).closest($('.filter-dropdown'));
 				var category = $element.data('filter');
 				
 				this.dom.eventsFilter.find('.dropdown').remove();
 				
 				if(!$element.hasClass('active')) {
 					// remove active from both dropdown buttons
 					this.dom.dropdownButtons.removeClass('active');
 					// add active to THIS dropdown button
 					$element.addClass('active');
 					// Add dropdown menu
 					this.dom.eventsFilter.append(this.filtersListTemplate(this.filters[category]));
 				
 				} else {
 					this.dom.dropdownButtons.removeClass('active');
 				}
 				
 				return false;
 			},
 			
 			onFilterChoiceClick: function(event) {
 				event.preventDefault();
 				var $element = $(event.target).closest('.filter-choice');
 				var category = $element.closest($('.events-filter')).find($('.filter-dropdown.active')).data('filter');
 				var choice = $element.data('name');
 				var filter = _.find(this.filters[category], 'name', choice);
 				
 				$element.toggleClass('checked');
 				
 				if (filter.checked) {
 					filter.checked = false
 					_.pull(this.activeFilters[category], filter.name);
 				} else {
 					filter.checked = true;
 					this.activeFilters[category].push(filter.name);
 				}
 				this.displayEvents();
 				return false;
 			},
 			resize : function(event, data) {
 				//display calendar if is visible
 				var displayCalendar = (this.dom.calendarContainer.css("display") == "none" ? false : true);
 				if (this.currentCalendar.displayCalendar != displayCalendar)
 				{
 					//view of calendar has changed
 					this.currentCalendar.displayCalendar = displayCalendar;
 					if (this.currentCalendar.displayCalendar)
 					{
 						this.currentCalendar.calendarObject.fullCalendar('render');
 						this.styleCalendar();
 					}
 				}
 			},
 			styleCalendar: function() {
 				// Update each cell with background color according to number of events
 				this.dom.allCalendarTDs = this.dom.calendar.find('.fc-day-number');
 				if (this.dom.allCalendarTDs.length == 0)
 					return 0;
 				
 				for(var j = 0; j < this.currentCalendar.numDays; j++) {
 					var targetCell = this.dom.allCalendarTDs.eq(j);
 					var targetDate = moment(targetCell.data('date'));
 					var thatDaysEvents = _.where(this.currentCalendar.events, {
 						dateStr: targetDate.format('YYYY-MM-DD')
 					});
 					thatDaysEvents = Math.min( Math.max( thatDaysEvents.length, 0 ), 5 );
 					targetCell.addClass('fc-events-count-' + thatDaysEvents);
 				}
 				
 				//select today or first day of the month
 				var dayToSelect = this.dom.allCalendarTDs.filter(".fc-today");
 				if (dayToSelect.length == 0)
 					dayToSelect = this.dom.allCalendarTDs.filter(':not(".fc-other-month"):first');
 				dayToSelect.addClass('fc-selected-date');
 			},
 			checkDisplayState : function() {
 				//check do we need to display Empty Text
 				if (this.div.find('.event:not(.hide)').length == 0)
 				{
 					this.dom.eventsContainer.addClass("hide");
 					this.dom.noData.removeClass("hide");
 				}else{
 					this.dom.eventsContainer.removeClass("hide");
 					this.dom.noData.addClass("hide");
 				}
 			},
 			dayClick: function(event) {
 				console.log(this.label() + ' day click');
 				
 				var targetDateStr = event.format('YYYY-MM-DD');
 				this.selectedDate = targetDateStr;
 				this.dom.allCalendarTDs.removeClass('fc-selected-date');
 				this.dom.allCalendarTDs.filter('[data-date="' + targetDateStr + '"]').addClass('fc-selected-date');
 				this.displayEvents();
 			},
 			viewRender: function(event) {
 				console.log(this.label() + ' view render', event);
 				
 				//calendar start interval
 				var startMoment = event.intervalStart.clone();
 				var startDate = startMoment.add((new Date(startMoment).getTimezoneOffset())/60, 'hour').clone();
 				//current start interval
 				startMoment = this.currentCalendar.start.clone();
 				var currentStartDate = startMoment.add((new Date(startMoment).getTimezoneOffset())/60, 'hour').clone();	
 				if (startDate.format('MM') == currentStartDate.format('MM')) return 0; // same month, already have the data
 				
 				// Get info about the month
 				this.dom.mobileCalendarToggle.find('.date-container').text(event.intervalStart.format('MMMM YYYY'));
 				this.currentCalendar.start = event.intervalStart; //( event.intervalStart < moment() ? moment() : event.intervalStart );
 				this.currentCalendar.end = event.intervalEnd;
 				this.currentCalendar.numDays = Math.floor(this.currentCalendar.end.diff(this.currentCalendar.start) / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24));
 				
 				this.callForEvents();
 			},
 			
 			loadMore: function(event) {
 				event.preventDefault();
 				this.displayEvents({showAll:true});
 			},
 			onMobileCalendarToggleClick: function(event) {
 				if (event) {
 					event.preventDefault();
 				}
 				this.dom.body.toggleClass('modal-mobile-calendar');
 				if ((this.dom.allCalendarTDs != null) && (this.dom.allCalendarTDs.length == 0)) {
 					this.currentCalendar.calendarObject.fullCalendar('render');
 					this.styleCalendar();
 				}
 				return false;
 			},
 			onKeyUp: _.throttle(function(event) {
 				var time = 0;
 				
 				// If pasting, set small delay to allow time for system to paste
 				if (event.type === 'paste') {
 					time = 200;
 				
 				// if enter key is pressed, unfocus input and close mobile calendar  
 				} else if (event.keyCode === 13){
 					this.dom.filterInput.blur();
 					if (this.dom.body.hasClass('modal-mobile-calendar')) {
 						$.proxy(this.onMobileCalendarToggleClick(null), this);
 					}
 				}
 				
 				window.setTimeout($.proxy(function(){
 					this.filterString = this.dom.filterInput.val().toLowerCase();
 					this.displayEvents();
 				}, this), time);
 			}, 300),
 			eventFilter: function(eventObj, options){
 				
 				var result = true;
 				
 				// is event on or after selected date?
 				if (eventObj.moment.isBefore(this.selectedDate, 'day')) {
 					result = false;
 				}
 				// does event match search string?
 				if (this.filterString) {
 					if (eventObj.lead === undefined) {
 						eventObj.lead = '';
 					}
 					
 					if (eventObj.name.toLowerCase().indexOf(this.filterString) === -1 && eventObj.lead.toLowerCase().indexOf(this.filterString) === -1) {
 						result = false;
 					}
 				}
 				// does event match the dropdown filters?
 				_.forEach(this.activeFilters, function(value, key){
 					// If no options are passed in, continue
 					// If there are options, check if options[key] is true to continue
 					if (!options || options[key]) {
 						if (value.indexOf(eventObj[key.slice(0, -1)]) === -1) {
 							result = false;
 						}
 					}
 				});
 				
 				// PASSED ALL FILTERS!
 				return result;
 			},
 			initAddToCalendar: function(){
 				// Venue Handles for Stanza iframe
 				var $calendarButtons = $('.add-to-calendar');
 				
 				// Select all 'add-to-calendar' buttons
 				$calendarButtons.map($.proxy(function(index, element){
 					var $element = $(element);
 					var venue = $element.closest('[data-venue]').data('venue');
 					// give it a data-handle based on closest data-venue
 					$element.attr('data-handle', this.venueHandles[venue] || this.venueHandles['default']);
 				}, this));
 			}
 		});
 	};
 	return tmpModule;
 });
 define('noop', [], function() {
 	function tmpModule(defaults) {
 		Module.call(this, {
 			mod: 'noop',
 			postProcess: function() {
 				console.log(this.label(), 'Post Process', this);
 			}
 		});
 	}
 	return tmpModule;
 });
   </script>
   <script id="tray-template" type="text/x-handlebars">
    {{#if data.addModuleContainer}}
 <div class="generic-module layout-module" data-module-id="{{id}}">
 {{/if}}
 
 {{#unless data.items}}
 
 <!-- Tray: "{{title}}" has no data items to display -->
 {{else}}
 
 <div class="content-container tray {{data.type}} {{#if data.showTitle}}show-title{{/if}} {{#if data.hideTop}}hide-top{{/if}}">
 
 	<div class="tray-top">
 		<h2>
 			<span class="heading-text">{{title}}</span>
 			{{#if data.link}}
 				<a href="{{data.link.url}}" class="tray-external-link">{{data.link.title}} {{{svgIcon "icon-arrow-right"}}}</a>
 			{{/if}}
 			{{#if data.seeAllLink}}
 				<span class="see-all-link" data-collapsed-text="See all {{length data.items}} {{{escape (svgIcon "icon-arrow-right")}}}">See all {{length data.items}} {{{svgIcon "icon-arrow-right"}}}</span>
 			{{/if}}
 		</h2>
 	{{#if data.sorting}}
 		<div class="controls">
 			<p class="sort-controls">
 				<span class="sort active" data-sort="{{data.sorting.method}}">{{data.sorting.label}}</span>
 			</p>
 		</div>
 	{{/if}}
 		<div class="counts">
 			<div class="snag-pager">
 				<span class="page-num">1</span>
 				<span class="num-items">{{length data.items}}</span>
 			</div>
 		</div>
 	</div>
 	
 	{{#if data.blurb}}
 		<p class="tray-description no-margin">{{{data.blurb}}}</p>
 	{{/if}}
 	
 	<div class="snag-slider-container {{#if data.expanded}}expanded{{/if}}">
 		<span class="prev disabled">{{{svgIcon "icon-arrow-left"}}}</span>
 		<div class="snag-slider {{#if data.sorting}}mixitup-container{{/if}}" data-heading="{{title}}">
 {{#with data}}
 		{{#each items}}
 			<div class="snag-slider-item {{additionalItemClassName}}" 
 				data-film-id="{{id}}" 
 				data-content-id="{{id}}" 
 				data-type="{{type}}"
 				data-title="{{title}}" 
 				data-description="{{description}}" 
 				data-year="{{year}}" 
 				data-runtime="{{runtime}}" 
 				data-permalink="{{permalink}}"
 			
 				{{#if ../sorting ~}}
 					data-{{getFirstDefinedValue ../sorting.method @root.data.sorting.method}}="{{@index}}"
 				{{~/if}}
 				>
 				
 				{{#compare type "film"}}
 					{{> collections/components/film/monumental-network trayType=(getTraySlideImageSize imageOverridden ../../trayType ../../config.defaultTrayType)}}
 				{{/compare}}
 				
 				{{#compare type "event"}}
 					{{> collections/components/event/monumental-network}}
 				{{/compare}}
 				
 				{{#compare type "article"}}
 					{{> collections/components/article/monumental-network}}
 				{{/compare}}
 				
 				{{#compare type "sportsPlayer"}}
 					{{> collections/components/player/monumental-network}}
 				{{/compare}}
 				
 				{{#compare type "merchandise"}}
 					{{> collections/components/merchandise/monumental-network}}
 				{{/compare}}
 				
 				{{#compare type "tag"}}
 					{{> collections/components/tag/monumental-network}}
 				{{/compare}}
 				
 			</div>
 			
 		{{/each}}
 		</div>
 		<span class="next">{{{svgIcon "icon-arrow-right"}}}</span>
 	</div>
 </div>
 {{/with}}
 
 {{/unless}}
 
 {{#if data.addModuleContainer}}
 </div>
 {{/if}}
   </script>
   <script id="login-template" type="text/x-handlebars">
    <div class="login-container">
 	<h1 class="user-auth-heading">Sign In</h1>
 	<div class="auth-types-container">
 		<div class="site-auth">
 			<form action="#" method="post" name="register">
 				<p>
 					<input class="large" type="email" required name="email" placeholder="Your Email Address" />
 					<label for="email" style="display: none;"></label>
 				</p>
 				<p>
 					<input class="large" type="password" required name="password" placeholder="Enter Your Password" />
 					<label for="password" style="display: none;"></label>
 				</p>
 				<p>
 					<input type="checkbox" checked name="rememberMe" /> Remember Me
 				</p>
 				<p>
 					<button class="large color-site" type="submit">Sign In</button>
 				</p>
